<analysis>**original_problem_statement:**
The user's goal is to create a production-ready P2P crypto exchange platform on the TON blockchain. The initial specification required PostgreSQL for financial data, but the current implementation uses MongoDB.

Throughout the session, the user's requirements evolved to include:
1.  **Real-world financial operations:** The system must handle real USDT deposits and withdrawals on the TON mainnet, including transaction hash tracking.
2.  **Simplified User Experience:** Replace long UUIDs for deposit comments with short, 6-digit numerical codes.
3.  **Advanced Admin Controls:**
    *   Implement a Trusted User feature to allow specific users to withdraw funds without manual admin approval.
    *   Provide the admin with a comprehensive history of all deposits and withdrawals on the platform.
    *   Allow the admin to generate a new hot wallet and securely view the seed phrase one time for backup.
    *   Enable the admin to perform manual withdrawals of both TON and USDT directly from the hot wallet.
4.  **Database Management:** A request to wipe the database and create a clean slate with specific users.

**User's preferred language**: Russian

**what currently exists?**
The application is a full-stack React/FastAPI/MongoDB platform. The  (Node.js) is configured for **mainnet** and now handles real-time USDT deposit detection by listening to the hot wallet's transactions.

-   **Backend:** The financial logic has been significantly enhanced.
    -   : Withdrawal logic was updated to support Trusted Users by automatically setting their withdrawal status to .
    -   : Now includes endpoints for viewing deposit/withdrawal history, managing the hot wallet (generation, withdrawal), and toggling a user's trusted status.
    -   : User registration now generates a unique, 6-digit .

-   **Frontend:**
    -   : The admin dashboard has been expanded with tabs for Withdrawal History and Deposit History. It also features a robust Wallet Management section for generating wallets (with a one-time seed phrase display) and performing manual withdrawals.
    -   : A Trusted toggle (shield icon) has been added to the user list, allowing the admin to manage withdrawal permissions.
    -   : The withdrawal modal UI has been fixed to clearly communicate how the commission is applied (added on top of the amount, not subtracted from it), resolving a major point of user confusion.

-   **:**
    -   : Completely refactored to use MongoDB instead of PostgreSQL for fetching user data and crediting balances. It now listens for USDT deposits and identifies users via the short  in the transaction comment.
    -   : A  has been added to mitigate rate-limiting issues.

The agent was about to start investigating the  logs to diagnose the failure in the automatic deposit crediting logic.
